set object rectangle from   4, 99 to   5,100 fc rgb "black"
set object rectangle from   3, 99 to   4,100 fc rgb "white"
set object rectangle from   2, 99 to   3,100 fc rgb "white"
set object rectangle from   1, 99 to   2,100 fc rgb "white"
set object rectangle from   0, 99 to   1,100 fc rgb "black"
plot 1
quit
